style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JNROLI+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当在资产负债表日按照未到期责任负债</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JNROLI+FangSong_GB2312">与已发生赔款负债之和对保险合同负债进行后续计量。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JNROLI+FangSong_GB2312">未到期责任负债包括资产负债表日分摊至保险合同组的、与未</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JNROLI+FangSong_GB2312">到期责任有关的履约现金流量和当日该合同组的合同服务边际。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JNROLI+FangSong_GB2312">已发生赔款负债包括资产负债表日分摊至保险合同组的、与已</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">发生赔案及其他相关费用有关的履约现金流量。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第二十九条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">对于不具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同组，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">资产负债表日合同组的合同服务边际账面价值应当以期初账面价值</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">为基础，经下列各项调整后予以确定：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">（一）当期归入该合同组的合同对合同服务边际的影响金额；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">（二）合同服务边际在当期计提的利息，计息利率为该合同组</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">内合同确认时、不随基础项目回报变动的现金流量所适用的加权平</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">均利率；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">（三）与未来服务相关的履约现金流量的变动金额，但履约现</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">金流量增加额超过合同服务边际账面价值所导致的亏损部分，以及</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">履约现金流量减少额抵销的未到期责任负债的亏损部分除外；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">（四）合同服务边际在当期产生的汇兑差额；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">（五）合同服务边际在当期的摊销金额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当按照提供保险合同服务的模式，合理确</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">定合同组在责任期内各个期间的责任单元，并据此对根据本准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">二十九条（一）至（四）调整后的合同服务边际账面价值进行摊销，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">计入当期及以后期间保险服务收入。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十一条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">企业因当期提供保险合同服务导致未到期责任</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">负债账面价值的减少额，应当确认为保险服务收入；因当期发生赔案及其他相关费用导致已发生赔款负债账面价值的增加额，以及与</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">之相关的履约现金流量的后续变动额，应当确认为保险服务费用。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">企业在确认保险服务收入和保险服务费用时，不得包含保险合</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MEMVIR+FangSong_GB2312">同中的投资成分。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十二条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当将合同组内的保险获取现金流量，随时</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">间流逝进行系统摊销，计入责任期内各个期间的保险服务费用，同</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">时确认为保险服务收入，以反映该类现金流量所对应的保费的收回。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十三条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当将货币时间价值及金融风险的影响导</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">致的未到期责任负债和已发生赔款负债账面价值变动额，作为保险</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">合同金融变动额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">企业可以选择将货币时间价值及金融风险的影响导致的非金融</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">风险调整变动额不作为保险合同金融变动额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十四条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当考虑持有的相关资产及其会计处理，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">在合同组合层面对保险合同金融变动额的会计处理做出下列会计政</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">策选择：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">（一）将保险合同金融变动额全额计入当期保险财务损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">（二）将保险合同金融变动额分解计入当期保险财务损益和其他</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">综合收益。选择该会计政策的，企业应当在合同组剩余期限内，采用系统合理的方法确定计入各个期间保险财务损益的金额，其与保</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">险合同金融变动额的差额计入其他综合收益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">保险财务损益，是指计入当期及以后期间损益的保险合同金融</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">变动额。保险财务损益包括企业签发的保险合同的承保财务损益和</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">分出的再保险合同的分出再保险财务损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十五条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当将非金融风险调整账面价值变动中除</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">保险合同金融变动额以外的金额计入当期及以后期间损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十六条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">对于本准则适用范围内的具有相机参与分红特</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: TFWQEB+FangSong_GB2312">征的投资合同，企业应当按照本准则有关保险合同的规定进行会计处</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">理，但下列各项特殊规定除外：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">（一）初始确认的时点为企业成为合同一方的日期。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">（二）企业有支付现金的实质性义务的，该义务所产生的现金</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">流量在合同边界内。企业有实际能力对其支付现金的承诺进行重新定价以充分反映其承诺支付现金的金额及相关风险的，表明企业无</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">支付现金的实质性义务。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">（三）企业应当按照投资服务的提供模式，在合同组期限内采</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">用系统合理的方法对合同服务边际进行摊销，计入当期及以后期间</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.4pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十七条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">对于中期财务报表中根据本准则作出的相关会</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">计估计处理结果，企业应当就是否在本年度以后中期财务报表和年度财务报表中进行调整做出会计政策选择，并一致应用于本准则适</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">用范围内的合同组。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十八条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">企业对产生外币现金流量的合同组进行计量时，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">应当将保险合同负债视为货币性项目，根据《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">19</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">号</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HCFGNG+TimesNewRomanPSMT">——</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">外币折算》有关规定处理。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">资产负债表日，产生外币现金流量的合同组的汇兑差额应当计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">入当期损益。企业根据本准则第三十四条规定选择将保险合同金融变动额分解计入当期保险财务损益和其他综合收益的，与计入其他</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">综合收益的金额相关的汇兑差额，应当计入其他综合收益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WVODAI+KaiTi_GB2312">第二节</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 11.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WVODAI+KaiTi_GB2312">具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同组计量的特殊规定</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十九条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UKMDQG+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当在合同开始日评估一项合同是否为具</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">有直接参与分红特征的保险合同，后续不再重新评估。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四十条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同，是指在合同</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">开始日同时符合下列条件的保险合同：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">（一）合同条款规定保单持有人参与分享清晰可辨认的基础项</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">目；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">（二）企业预计将基础项目公允价值变动回报中的相当大部分</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">支付给保单持有人；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">（三）预计应付保单持有人金额变动中的相当大部分将随基础</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">项目公允价值的变动而变动。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四十一条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当按照基础项目公允价值扣除浮动收费</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">的差额，估计具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同组的履约现金流量。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">浮动收费，是指企业因代保单持有人管理基础项目并提供投资</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">相关服务而取得的对价，等于基础项目公允价值中企业享有份额减</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">去不随基础项目回报变动的履约现金流量。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四十二条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">对于具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同组，资</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">产负债表日合同组的合同服务边际账面价值应当以期初账面价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">基础，经下列调整后予以确定：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">（一）当期归入该合同组的合同对合同服务边际的影响金额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">（二）基础项目公允价值中企业享有份额的变动金额，但以下</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">情形除外：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">．企业使用衍生工具或分出再保险合同管理与该金额变动相关</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OCPFNK+FangSong_GB2312">金融风险时，对符合本准则规定条件的，可以选择将该金额变动中由货币时间价值及金融风险的影响导致的部分计入当期保险财务损</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">益。但企业将分出再保险合同的保险合同金融变动额分解计入当期保险财务损益和其他综合收益的，该金额变动中的相应部分也应予</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">以分解。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">．基础项目公允价值中企业享有份额的减少额超过合同服务边</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">际账面价值所导致的亏损部分。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">．基础项目公允价值中企业享有份额的增加额抵销的未到期责</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">任负债的亏损部分。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">（三）与未来服务相关且不随基础项目回报变动的履约现金流</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">量的变动金额，但以下情形除外：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">．企业使用衍生工具、分出再保险合同或以公允价值计量且其</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">变动计入当期损益的非衍生金融工具管理与该履约现金流量变动相关金融风险时，对符合本准则规定条件的，可以选择将该履约现金流量变动中由货币时间价值及金融风险的影响导致的部分计入当期保险财务损益。但企业将分出再保险合同的保险合同金融变动额分解计入当期保险财务损益和其他综合收益的，该履约现金流量变动</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">中的相应部分也应予以分解。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">．该履约现金流量的增加额超过合同服务边际账面价值所导致</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">的亏损部分。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">．该履约现金流量的减少额抵销的未到期责任负债的亏损部分。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">（四）合同服务边际在当期产生的汇兑差额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">（五）合同服务边际在当期的摊销金额。企业应当按照提供保</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RULLGT+FangSong_GB2312">险合同服务的模式，合理确定合同组在责任期内各个期间的责任单元，并据此对根据本条（一）至（四）调整后的合同服务边际账面</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">价值进行摊销，计入当期及以后期间保险服务收入。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">企业可以对本条（二）和（三）中的变动金额进行合并调整。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四十三条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">企业采用风险管理措施对具有直接参与分红特</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">征的保险合同产生的金融风险予以缓释时，同时符合下列条件的，对于本准则第四十二条（二）和（三）相关金额变动中由货币时间</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">价值及金融风险的影响导致的部分，可以选择不调整合同服务边际：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">（一）企业制定了关于风险管理目标和策略的书面文件；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">（二）保险合同与用于风险管理的衍生工具、分出再保险合同</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">或以公允价值计量且其变动计入当期损益的非衍生金融工具之间存</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">在经济抵销关系；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">（三）经济抵销关系产生的价值变动中，信用风险的影响不占</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">主导地位。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">企业不再符合上述条件时，应当自不符合之日起，将本准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">四十二条（二）和（三）相关金额变动中由货币时间价值及金融风险的影响导致的部分调整合同服务边际，之前已经计入保险财务损</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">益的金额不予调整。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四十四条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">对于企业不持有基础项目的具有直接参与分红</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">特征的保险合同组，企业应当根据本准则第三十四条规定，对保险</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">合同金额变动额进行会计处理。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CWSUVN+FangSong_GB2312">对于企业持有基础项目的具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同组，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">企业根据本准则第三十四条规定，选择将保险合同金融变动额分解</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">计入当期保险财务损益和其他综合收益的，计入当期保险财务损益的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">金额应当等于其持有的基础项目按照相关会计准则规定计入当期损</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">益的金额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">本准则第四十二条对保险合同金融变动额的会计处理另有规定</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">的，从其规定。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四十五条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">分入和分出的再保险合同不适用本节规定。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MFQQUR+KaiTi_GB2312">第三节</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 11.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: MFQQUR+KaiTi_GB2312">亏损保险合同组计量的特殊规定</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四十六条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">合同组在初始确认时发生首日亏损的，或合同</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">组合中的合同归入其所属亏损合同组而新增亏损的，企业应当确认亏损并计入当期保险服务费用，同时将该亏损部分增加未到期责任</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">负债账面价值。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">初始确认时，亏损合同组的保险合同负债账面价值等于其履约</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">现金流量。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四十七条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">发生下列情形之一导致合同组在后续计量时发</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">生亏损的，企业应当确认亏损并计入当期保险服务费用，同时将该</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">亏损部分增加未到期责任负债账面价值：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">（一）因与未来服务相关的未来现金流量或非金融风险调整的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">估计发生变更，导致履约现金流量增加额超过合同服务边际账面价</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">值。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">（二）对于具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同组，其基础项目</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">公允价值中企业享有份额的减少额超过合同服务边际账面价值。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四十八条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">企业在确认合同组的亏损后，应当将未到期责</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">任负债账面价值的下列变动额，采用系统合理的方法分摊至未到期</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPHRMI+FangSong_GB2312">责任负债中的亏损部分和其他部分：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">（一）因发生保险服务费用而减少的未来现金流量的现值；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">（二）因相关风险释放而计入当期损益的非金融风险调整的变</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">动金额；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">（三）保险合同金融变动额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">分摊至亏损部分的金额不得计入当期保险服务收入。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四十九条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">企业在确认合同组的亏损后，应当按照下列规</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">定进行后续计量：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">（一）将因与未来服务相关的未来现金流量或非金融风险调整</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">的估计变更所导致的履约现金流量增加额，以及具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同组的基础项目公允价值中企业享有份额的减少额，确认为新增亏损并计入当期保险服务费用，同时将该亏损部分增加</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">未到期责任负债账面价值。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">（二）将因与未来服务相关的未来现金流量或非金融风险调整</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">的估计变更所导致的履约现金流量减少额，以及具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同组的基础项目公允价值中企业享有份额的增加额，减少未到期责任负债的亏损部分，冲减当期保险服务费用；超出亏</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">损部分的金额，确认为合同服务边际。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CTVWKF+KaiTi_GB2312">第四节</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 11.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: CTVWKF+KaiTi_GB2312">保险合同组计量的简化处理规定</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第五十条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">符合下列条件之一的，企业可以采用保费分配法</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">简化合同组的计量：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">（一）企业能够合理预计采用本节简化处理规定与根据本准则</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NLHKCH+FangSong_GB2312">前述章节规定计量合同组未到期责任负债的结果无重大差异。企业</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">预计履约现金流量在赔案发生前将发生重大变化的，表明该合同组</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">不符合本条件。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">（二）该合同组内各项合同的责任期不超过一年。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第五十一条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">企业对其签发的保险合同采用保费分配法时，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">应当假设初始确认时该合同所属合同组合内不存在亏损合同，该假</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">设与相关事实和情况不符的除外。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第五十二条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">企业采用保费分配法时，合同组内各项合同初</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">始确认时的责任期均不超过一年的，可以选择在保险获取现金流量</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">发生时将其确认为费用，计入当期损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第五十三条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">企业采用保费分配法计量合同组时，初始确认</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">时未到期责任负债账面价值等于已收保费减去初始确认时发生的保险获取现金流量（根据本准则第五十二条规定选择在发生时计入当期损益的除外），减去（或加上）在合同组初始确认时终止确认的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">保险获取现金流量资产以及其他相关资产或负债的金额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">资产负债表日未到期责任负债账面价值等于期初账面价值加上</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">当期已收保费，减去当期发生的保险获取现金流量（根据本准则第五十二条规定选择在发生时计入当期损益的除外），加上当期确认为保险服务费用的保险获取现金流量摊销金额和针对融资成分的调整金额，减去因当期提供保险合同服务而确认为保险服务收入的金</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">额和当期已付或转入已发生赔款负债中的投资成分。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第五十四条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">合同组内的合同中存在重大融资成分的，企业应</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">当按照合同组初始确认时确定的折现率，对未到期责任负债账面价</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NBDEAT+FangSong_GB2312">值进行调整，以反映货币时间价值及金融风险的影响。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">合同组初始确认时，如果企业预计提供保险合同服务每一部分</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">服务的时点与相关保费到期日之间的间隔不超过一年，可以不考虑</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">合同中存在的重大融资成分。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.4pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第五十五条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">相关事实和情况表明合同组在责任期内存在亏</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">损时，企业应当将该日与未到期责任相关的履约现金流量超过按照本准则第五十三条确定的未到期责任负债账面价值的金额，计入当</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">期保险服务费用，同时增加未到期责任负债账面价值。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第五十六条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当根据与已发生赔案及其他相关费用有</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">关的履约现金流量计量已发生赔款负债。相关履约现金流量预计在赔案发生后一年内支付或收取的，企业可以不考虑货币时间价值及金融风险的影响，且一致应用于本准则第五十五条规定的相关履约</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">现金流量的计算。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第五十七条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当将已收和预计收取的保费，在扣除投</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">资成分并根据本准则第五十四条规定对重大融资成分进行调整后，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">分摊至当期的金额确认为保险服务收入。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当随时间流逝在责任期内分摊经调整的已收和预计收取</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">的保费；保险合同的风险在责任期内不随时间流逝为主释放的，应</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">当以保险服务费用预计发生时间为基础进行分摊。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第六章</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 11.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">分出的再保险合同组的确认和计量</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第五十八条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">企业对分出的再保险合同组进行确认和计量，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: JEUHPN+FangSong_GB2312">除本章另有规定外，应当按照本准则有关保险合同的其他相关规定进行处理，但本准则第五章关于亏损合同组计量的相关规定不适用</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">于分出的再保险合同组。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第五十九条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当将同一分出的再保险合同组合至少分</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">为下列合同组：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">（一）初始确认时存在净利得的合同组；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">（二）初始确认时无显著可能性在未来产生净利得的合同组；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">（三）该组合中剩余合同组成的合同组。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">企业可以按照净成本或净利得水平以及初始确认后在未来产生</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">净利得的可能性等，对分出的再保险合同组作进一步细分。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">企业不得将分出时间间隔超过一年的合同归入同一分出的再保</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">险合同组。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第六十条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当在下列时点中的最早时点确认其分出的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">再保险合同组：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US
