style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">（一）分出的再保险合同组责任期开始日；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">（二）分出的再保险合同组所对应的保险合同组确认为亏损合</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">同组时。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第六十一条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">分出的再保险合同组分出成比例责任的，企业</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">应当在下列时点中的最早时点确认该合同组：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">（一）分出的再保险合同组责任期开始日和任一对应的保险合</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">同初始确认时点中较晚的时点；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">（二）分出的再保险合同组所对应的保险合同组确认为亏损合</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">同组时。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第六十二条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">企业在初始确认其分出的再保险合同组时，应</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DJDNBT+FangSong_GB2312">当按照履约现金流量与合同服务边际之和对分出再保险合同资产进</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">行初始计量。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">分出再保险合同组的合同服务边际，是指企业为在未来获得再</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">保险分入人提供的保险合同服务而产生的净成本或净利得。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第六十三条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">企业在估计分出的再保险合同组的未来现金流</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">量现值时，采用的相关假设应当与计量所对应的保险合同组保持一</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">致，并考虑再保险分入人的不履约风险。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第六十四条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当根据分出的再保险合同组转移给再保</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">险分入人的风险，估计非金融风险调整。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第六十五条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当在分出的再保险合同组初始确认时计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">算下列各项之和：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">（一）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 5.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">履约现金流量；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">（二）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 5.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">在该日终止确认的相关资产或负债对应的现金流量；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">（三）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 5.75pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">分出再保险合同组内合同在该日产生的现金流量；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">（四）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 5.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">分保摊回未到期责任资产亏损摊回部分的金额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当将上述各项之和所反映的净成本或净利得，确认为合</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">同服务边际。净成本与分出前发生的事项相关的，企业应当将其确</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">认为费用并计入当期损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第六十六条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当在资产负债表日按照分保摊回未到期</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">责任资产与分保摊回已发生赔款资产之和对分出再保险合同资产进</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">行后续计量。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">分保摊回未到期责任资产包括资产负债表日分摊至分出的再保</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">险合同组的、与未到期责任有关的履约现金流量和当日该合同组的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EBTNDG+FangSong_GB2312">合同服务边际。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">分保摊回已发生赔款资产包括资产负债表日分摊至分出的再保</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">险合同组的、与已发生赔款及其他相关费用的摊回有关的履约现金</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">流量。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第六十七条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">对于订立时点不晚于对应的保险合同确认时点</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">的分出的再保险合同，企业在初始确认对应的亏损合同组或者将对应的亏损保险合同归入合同组而确认亏损时，应当根据下列两项的乘积确定分出再保险合同组分保摊回未到期责任资产亏损摊回部分</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">的金额：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">（一）对应的保险合同确认的亏损；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">（二）预计从分出再保险合同组摊回的对应的保险合同赔付的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">比例。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当按照上述亏损摊回部分的金额调整分出再保险合同组</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">的合同服务边际，同时确认为摊回保险服务费用，计入当期损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">企业在对分出的再保险合同组进行后续计量时，应当调整亏损</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">摊回部分的金额以反映对应的保险合同亏损部分的变化，调整后的亏损摊回部分的金额不应超过企业预计从分出再保险合同组摊回的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">对应的保险合同亏损部分的相应金额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第六十八条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">资产负债表日分出的再保险合同组的合同服务</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">边际账面价值应当以期初账面价值为基础，经下列各项调整后予以确</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">定：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">（一）当期归入该合同组的合同对合同服务边际的影响金额；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">（二）合同服务边际在当期计提的利息，计息利率为该合同组</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OAPLPC+FangSong_GB2312">内合同确认时、不随基础项目回报变动的现金流量所适用的加权平</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">均利率；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">（三）根据本准则第六十七条第一款计算的分保摊回未到期责任资产亏损摊回部分的金额，以及与分出再保险合同组的履约现金</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">流量变动无关的分保摊回未到期责任资产亏损摊回部分的转回；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">（四）与未来服务相关的履约现金流量的变动金额，但分摊至对</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">应的保险合同组且不调整其合同服务边际的履约现金流量变动而导致的变动，以及对应的保险合同组采用保费分配法计量时因确认或</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">转回亏损而导致的变动除外；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">（五）合同服务边际在当期产生的汇兑差额；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">（六）合同服务边际在当期的摊销金额。企业应当按照取得保</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">险合同服务的模式，合理确定分出再保险合同组在责任期内各个期间的责任单元，并据此对根据本条（一）至（五）调整后的合同服</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">务边际账面价值进行摊销，计入当期及以后期间损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第六十九条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">再保险分入人不履约风险导致的履约现金流量</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">变动金额与未来服务无关，企业不应当因此调整分出再保险合同组</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">的合同服务边际。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第七十条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">企业因当期取得再保险分入人提供的保险合同服</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">务而导致分保摊回未到期责任资产账面价值的减少额，应当确认为分出保费的分摊；因当期发生赔款及其他相关费用的摊回导致分保摊回已发生赔款资产账面价值的增加额，以及与之相关的履约现金</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">流量的后续变动额，应当确认为摊回保险服务费用。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当将预计从再保险分入人收到的不取决于对应的保险合</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HFHMDH+FangSong_GB2312">同赔付的金额，作为分出保费的分摊的减项。企业在确认分出保费</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">的分摊和摊回保险服务费用时，不得包含分出再保险合同中的投资</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">成分。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第七十一条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">符合下列条件之一的，企业可以采用保费分配法</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">简化分出的再保险合同组的计量：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">（一）企业能够合理预计采用保费分配法与不采用保费分配法</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">计量分出再保险合同组的结果无重大差异。企业预计履约现金流量</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">在赔案发生前将发生重大变化的，表明该合同组不符合本条件。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">（二）该分出的再保险合同组内各项合同的责任期不超过一年。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第七十二条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">企业采用保费分配法计量分出的再保险合同组</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">时，根据本准则第六十七条第一款计算的亏损摊回部分的金额应当调整分出再保险合同组的分保摊回未到期责任资产账面价值，同时</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">确认为摊回保险服务费用，计入当期损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第七章</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 11.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">合同转让或非同一控制下企业合并中取得的保险合同的确认和计量</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第七十三条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">企业对合同转让或非同一控制下企业合并中取</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">得的保险合同进行确认和计量，除本章另有规定外，应当适用本准</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">则其他相关规定。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第七十四条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">企业在合同转让或非同一控制下企业合并中取</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">得的保险合同，应当视为在转让日（或购买日）订立该合同，并根</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">据本准则相关规定将该合同归入其所属合同组。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第七十五条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">企业在合同转让或非同一控制下企业合并中为</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: NOFSUE+FangSong_GB2312">取得保险合同而收到或支付的对价，应当视为收取或支付的保费。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第七十六条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">企业在合同转让或非同一控制下企业合并中取</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">得保险合同的会计处理适用《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
20</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">号</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SPUTAC+TimesNewRomanPSMT">——</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">企业合并》等其他会计准则的，应当根据相关会计准则进行处理。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第八章</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 11.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">保险合同的修改和终止确认</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第七十七条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">保险合同条款的修改符合下列条件之一的，企</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">业应当终止确认原合同，并按照修改后的合同条款确认一项新合同：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">（一）假设修改后的合同条款自合同开始日适用，出现下列情</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">形之一的：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">．修改后的合同不属于本准则的适用范围。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">．修改后的合同应当予以分拆且分拆后适用本准则的组成部</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">分发生变化。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">．修改后的合同的合同边界发生实质性变化。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">．修改后的合同归属于不同的合同组。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">（二）原合同与修改后的合同仅有其一符合具有直接参与分红</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">特征的保险合同的定义。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">（三）原合同采用保费分配法，修改后的合同不符合采用保费</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">分配法的条件。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">保险合同条款的修改不符合上述条件的，企业应当将合同条款</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">修改导致的现金流量变动作为履约现金流量的估计变更进行处理。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第七十八条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">保险合同约定的义务因履行、取消或到期而解</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">除的，企业应当终止确认保险合同。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第七十九条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: SASDBM+FangSong_GB2312">企业终止确认一项保险合同，应当按照下列规</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">定进行处理：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">（一）调整该保险合同所属合同组的履约现金流量，扣除与终</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">止确认的权利义务相关的未来现金流量现值和非金融风险调整。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">（二）调整合同组的合同服务边际。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">（三）调整合同组在当期及以后期间的责任单元。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第八十条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">企业修改原合同并确认新合同时，应当按照下列</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">两项的差额调整原合同所属合同组的合同服务边际：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">（一）因终止确认原合同所导致的合同组履约现金流量变动金</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">额；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">（二）修改日订立与新合同条款相同的合同预计将收取的保费</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">减去因修改原合同而收取的额外保费后的保费净额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">企业在计量新合同所属合同组时，应当假设于修改日收到本条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">（二）中的保费净额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第八十一条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">企业因合同转让而终止确认一项保险合同的，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">应当按照因终止确认该合同所导致的合同组履约现金流量变动金额与受让方收取的保费之间的差额，调整该合同所属合同组的合同服</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">务边际。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第八十二条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">企业因合同修改或转让而终止确认一项保险合</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">同时，应当将与该合同相关的、由于会计政策选择而在以前期间确认为其他综合收益的余额转入当期损益；但对于企业持有基础项目的具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同，企业不得仅因终止确认该保</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: LJSJLV+FangSong_GB2312">险合同而进行上述会计处理。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第九章</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 11.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">列报</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WMKMPB+KaiTi_GB2312">第一节</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 11.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WMKMPB+KaiTi_GB2312">资产负债表和利润表相关项目的列示及披露</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第八十三条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当根据自身实际情况，合理确定列报保</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">险合同的详细程度，避免列报大量不重要信息或不恰当汇总实质性</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">不同信息。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">企业可以按照合同类型、地理区域或报告分部等对保险合同的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">信息披露进行恰当汇总。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第八十四条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当在资产负债表中分别列示与保险合同</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">有关的下列项目：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">（一）保险合同资产；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">（二）保险合同负债；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">（三）分出再保险合同资产；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">（四）分出再保险合同负债。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">企业签发的保险合同组合账面价值为借方余额的，列示为保险</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">合同资产；分出的再保险合同组合账面价值为贷方余额的，列示为</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">分出再保险合同负债。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">保险获取现金流量资产于资产负债表日的账面价值应当计入保</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">险合同组合账面价值。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第八十五条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当在利润表中分别列示与保险合同有关</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">的下列项目：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">（一）保险服务收入；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VIHAPP+FangSong_GB2312">（二）保险服务费用；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">（三）分出保费的分摊；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">（四）摊回保险服务费用；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">（五）承保财务损益；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">（六）分出再保险财务损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第八十六条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当在附注中分别就签发的保险合同和分</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">出的再保险合同，单独披露未到期责任负债（或分保摊回未到期责任资产）和已发生赔款负债（或分保摊回已发生赔款资产）余额调</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">节表，以反映与保险合同账面价值变动有关的下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">（一）保险合同负债和保险合同资产（或分出再保险合同资产</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">和分出再保险合同负债）的期初和期末余额及净额，及净额调节情</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">况；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">（二）未到期责任负债（或分保摊回未到期责任资产）当期变</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">动情况，亏损部分（或亏损摊回部分）应单独披露；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">（三）已发生赔款负债（或分保摊回已发生赔款资产）当期变</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">动情况，采用保费分配法的保险合同应分别披露未来现金流量现值</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">和非金融风险调整；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">（四）当期保险服务收入；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">（五）当期保险服务费用，包括当期发生赔款及其他相关费用、</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">保险获取现金流量的摊销、亏损部分的确认及转回和已发生赔款负</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">债相关履约现金流量变动；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">（六）当期分出保费的分摊；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">（七）当期摊回保险服务费用，包括摊回当期发生赔款及其他</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: BOKKOP+FangSong_GB2312">相关费用、亏损摊回部分的确认及转回和分保摊回已发生赔款资产</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">相关履约现金流量变动；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">（八）不计入当期损益的投资成分，保费返还可以在此项合并</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">披露；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">（九）与当期服务无关但影响保险合同账面价值的金额，包括</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">当期现金流量、再保险分入人不履约风险变动额、保险合同金融变动额、其他与保险合同账面价值变动有关的金额。当期现金流量应分别披露收到保费（或支付分出保费）、支付保险获取现金流量、</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">支付赔款及其他相关费用（或收到摊回赔款及其他相关费用）。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第八十七条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">对于未采用保费分配法的保险合同，企业应当</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">在附注中分别就签发的保险合同和分出的再保险合同，单独披露履约现金流量和合同服务边际余额调节表，以反映与保险合同账面价</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">值变动有关的下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">（一）保险合同负债和保险合同资产（或分出再保险合同资产</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">和分出再保险合同负债）的期初和期末余额及净额，及净额调节情</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">况；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">（二）未来现金流量现值当期变动情况；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">（三）非金融风险调整当期变动情况；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">（四）合同服务边际当期变动情况；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">（五）与当期服务相关的变动情况，包括合同服务边际的摊销、</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">非金融风险调整的变动、当期经验调整；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">（六）与未来服务相关的变动情况，包括当期初始确认的保险</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">合同影响金额、调整合同服务边际的估计变更、不调整合同服务边</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PBEQEB+FangSong_GB2312">际的估计变更；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">（七）与过去服务相关的变动情况，包括已发生赔款负债（或</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">分保摊回已发生赔款资产）相关履约现金流量变动；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">（八）与当期服务无关但影响保险合同账面价值的金额，包括</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">当期现金流量、再保险分入人不履约风险变动额、保险合同金融变动额、其他与保险合同账面价值变动有关的金额。当期现金流量应分别披露收到保费（或支付分出保费）、支付保险获取现金流量、</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">支付赔款及其他相关费用（或收到摊回赔款及其他相关费用）。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第八十八条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当在附注中披露关于保险获取现金流量</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">资产的下列定量信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle
