style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">（一）保险获取现金流量资产的期初和期末余额及其调节情况；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">（二）保险获取现金流量资产减值准备当期计提和当期转回情</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">况；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">（三）期末保险获取现金流量资产预计在未来按适当的时间段</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">终止确认的相关信息。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第八十九条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">对于未采用保费分配法的保险合同，企业应当</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">在附注中分别就签发的保险合同和分出的再保险合同，披露当期初</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">始确认的保险合同对资产负债表影响的下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">（一）未来现金流出现值，保险获取现金流量的金额应单独披</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">露；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">（二）未来现金流入现值；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">（三）非金融风险调整；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">（四）合同服务边际。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OTUFJS+FangSong_GB2312">对于当期初始确认的亏损合同组以及在合同转让或非同一控制</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">下企业合并中取得的保险合同，企业应当分别披露其对资产负债表</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">影响的上述信息。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第九十条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">对于未采用保费分配法的签发的保险合同，企业</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">应当在附注中披露与本期确认保险服务收入相关的下列定量信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">（一）与未到期责任负债变动相关的保险服务收入，分别披露期</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">初预计当期发生的保险服务费用、非金融风险调整的变动、合同服务边际的摊销、其他金额（如与当期服务或过去服务相关的保费经</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">验调整）；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">（二）保险获取现金流量的摊销。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第九十一条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">对于未采用保费分配法的保险合同，企业应当</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">在附注中分别就签发的保险合同和分出的再保险合同，披露期末合同服务边际在剩余期限内按适当的时间段摊销计入利润表的定量信</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">息。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第九十二条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当披露当期保险合同金融变动额的定量</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">信息及其解释性说明，包括对保险合同金融变动额与相关资产投资</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">回报关系的说明。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第九十三条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当披露与具有直接参与分红特征的保险</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">合同相关的下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">（一）基础项目及其公允价值；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">（二）根据本准则第四十二条和第四十三条规定，将货币时间</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">价值及金融风险的影响金额计入当期保险财务损益或其他综合收益</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">对当期合同服务边际的影响。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第九十四条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DUTJJH+FangSong_GB2312">对于具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同组，企业</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">选择将保险合同金融变动额分解计入当期保险财务损益和其他综合收益的，根据本准则第四十四条规定，因是否持有基础项目的情况发生变动导致计入当期保险财务损益的计量方法发生变更的，应当披露变更原因和对财务报表项目的影响金额，以及相关合同组在变</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">更日的账面价值。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PGGKUP+KaiTi_GB2312">第二节</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 11.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: PGGKUP+KaiTi_GB2312">与保险合同计量相关的披露</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第九十五条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当披露与保险合同计量所采用的方法、</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">输入值和假设等相关的下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">（一）保险合同计量所采用的方法以及估计相关输入值的程序。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当披露相关输入值的定量信息，不切实可行的除外。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">（二）本条（一）中所述方法和程序的变更及其原因，以及受</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">影响的合同类型。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">（三）与保险合同计量有关的下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">．对于不具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同，区分相机抉择</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">与其他因素导致未来现金流量估计变更的方法；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">．确定非金融风险调整的计量方法及计量结果所对应的置信</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">水平，以及非金融风险调整变动额根据本准则第三十三条在利润表</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">中的列示方法；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">．确定折现率的方法，以及用于不随基础项目回报变动的现金</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">流量折现的收益率曲线（或收益率曲线范围）；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">．确定投资成分的方法；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EITVII+FangSong_GB2312">．确定责任单元组成部分及相对权重的方法。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第九十六条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">企业选择将保险合同金融变动额分解计入当期</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">保险财务损益和其他综合收益的，应当披露确定保险财务损益金额</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">的方法及其说明。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第九十七条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">对于采用保费分配法计量的保险合同组，企业</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">应当披露下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">（一）合同组适用保费分配法的判断依据；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">（二）未到期责任负债（或分保摊回未到期责任资产）和已发</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">生赔款负债（或分保摊回已发生赔款资产）的计量是否反映货币时</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">间价值及金融风险的影响；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">（三）是否在保险获取现金流量发生时将其确认为费用。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UFLWDO+KaiTi_GB2312">第三节</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 11.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: UFLWDO+KaiTi_GB2312">与风险相关的披露</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第九十八条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当披露与保险合同产生的保险风险和金</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">融风险等相关的定性和定量信息。金融风险包括市场风险、信用风</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">险、流动性风险等。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第九十九条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">对于保险合同产生的各类风险，企业应当按类</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">别披露下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">（一）风险敞口及其形成原因，以及在本期发生的变化。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">（二）风险管理的目标、政策和程序以及计量风险的方法及其</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">在本期发生的变化。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">（三）期末风险敞口的汇总数据。该数据应当以向内部关键管</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">理人员提供的相关信息为基础。期末风险敞口不能反映企业本期风</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EHVSCB+FangSong_GB2312">险敞口变动情况的，企业应当进一步提供相关信息。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">（四）风险集中度信息，包括企业确定风险集中度的说明和参</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">考因素（如保险事项类型、行业特征、地理区域、货币种类等）。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当披露相关监管要求（如最低资本要求、</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">保证利率等）对本准则适用范围内的合同的影响。保险合同分组时</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">应用本准则第十五条规定的，企业应当披露这一事实。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百零一条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 23.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当对保险风险和市场风险进行敏感性</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">分析并披露下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">（一）资产负债表日保险风险变量和各类市场风险变量发生合</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">理、可能的变动时，将对企业损益和所有者权益产生的影响。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">对于保险风险，敏感性分析应当反映对企业签发的保险合同及</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">其经分出的再保险合同进行风险缓释后的影响。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">对于各类市场风险，敏感性分析应当反映保险合同所产生的风</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">险变量与企业持有的金融资产所产生的风险变量之间的关联性。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">（二）本期进行敏感性分析所使用的方法和假设，以及在本期</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">发生的变化及其原因。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百零二条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 23.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">企业为管理保险合同所产生的风险，采用不</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">同于本准则第一百零一条中所述方法进行敏感性分析的，应当披露</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">（一）用于敏感性分析的方法、选用的主要参数和假设；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">（二）所用方法的目的，以及该方法提供信息的局限性。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百零三条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 23.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当披露索赔进展情况，以反映已发生</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">赔款的实际赔付金额与未经折现的预计赔付金额的比较信息，及其</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: HIAKRP+FangSong_GB2312">与资产负债表日已发生赔款负债账面价值的调节情况。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">索赔进展情况的披露应当从赔付时间和金额在资产负债表日仍</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">存在不确定性的重大赔付最早发生期间开始，但最长披露期限可不超过十年。赔付时间和金额的不确定性在未来一年内将消除的索赔</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">进展信息可以不披露。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百零四条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当披露与保险合同所产生的信用风险</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">相关的下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">（一）签发的保险合同和分出的再保险合同分别于资产负债表</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">日的最大信用风险敞口；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">（二）与分出再保险合同资产的信用质量相关的信息。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百零五条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 23.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当披露与保险合同所产生的流动性风</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">险相关的下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">（一）对管理流动性风险的说明。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">（二）对资产负债表日保险合同负债和分出再保险合同负债的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">到期期限分析。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">到期期限分析应当基于合同组合，所使用的时间段至少应当为</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">资产负债表日后一年以内、一年至两年以内、两年至三年以内、三年至四年以内、四年至五年以内、五年以上。列入各时间段内的金额可</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">以是未来现金流量现值或者未经折现的合同剩余净现金流量。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">到期期限分析可以不包括采用保费分配法计量的保险合同负债</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">和分出再保险合同负债中与未到期责任相关的部分。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">（三）保单持有人可随时要求偿还的金额。企业应当说明该金</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EODGTM+FangSong_GB2312">额与相关保险合同组合账面价值之间的关联性。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第十章</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 11.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">衔接规定</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百零六条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 23.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">首次执行日之前的保险合同会计处理与本准</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">则规定不一致的，企业应当按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">28</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">号</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DTBUKU+TimesNewRomanPSMT">——</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">会计政<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">策、会计估计变更和差错更正》的规定采用追溯调整法处理，但本</SPAN>准则另有规定的除外。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">企业进行追溯调整的，无须披露当期和各个列报前期财务报表</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">受影响项目和每股收益的调整金额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百零七条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 23.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">企业采用追溯调整法时，应当在过渡日按照</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">下列规定进行衔接处理：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">（一）假设一直按照本准则要求识别、确认和计量保险合同组；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">（二）假设一直按照本准则要求识别、确认和计量保险获取现</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">金流量资产，但无须估计该资产于过渡日前的可收回金额；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">（三）确认追溯调整对所有者权益的累积影响数；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">（四）不得在过渡日前运用本准则第四十三条规定的风险管理</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">缓释选择权。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">过渡日是指本准则首次执行日前最近一个会计年度的期初，企</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">业列报经调整的更早期间的比较信息的，过渡日是更早比较期间的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">期初。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百零八条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 23.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">对合同组采用追溯调整法不切实可行的，企</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">业应当采用修正追溯调整法或公允价值法。对合同组采用修正追溯</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">调整法也不切实可行的，企业应当采用公允价值法。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: RJEBQW+FangSong_GB2312">修正追溯调整法，是指企业在对本章所涉及相关事项采用追溯</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">调整法不切实可行时，使用在过渡日无须付出不必要的额外成本或努力即可获得的合理可靠的信息，以获得接近追溯调整法结果为目</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">标，在衔接处理上按本准则规定进行简化的方法。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">公允价值法，是指以过渡日合同组公允价值与履约现金流量的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">差额确定合同组在该日的合同服务边际或未到期责任负债亏损部分，以及在衔接处理上按本准则规定进行简化的方法。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">企业在过渡日前符合本准则第四十三条规定条件，使用衍生工</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">具、分出的再保险合同或以公允价值计量且其变动计入当期损益的非衍生金融工具管理合同组产生的金融风险，并自过渡日起采用未来适用法运用风险管理缓释选择权进行会计处理的，企业可以对该</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">合同组采用公允价值法进行衔接处理。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百零九条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 23.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">企业采用修正追溯调整法时，应当在过渡日</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">根据本准则规定识别下列事项并进行衔接处理：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">（一）保险合同组，但在按照本准则规定进行保险合同分组时</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">无法获得合理可靠的信息的，企业可以将签发或分出时间间隔超过</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">一年的合同归入同一合同组；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">（二）具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">（三）不具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同中的相机抉择现金</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">流量；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">（四）具有相机参与分红特征的投资合同。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">企业采用修正追溯调整法时，对于在合同转让或非同一控制下企业合并中取得的保险合同，应当将该类合同在转让日或购买日前</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: WDJFTJ+FangSong_GB2312">已发生的赔付义务确认为已发生赔款负债。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百一十条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 23.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VWSHNM+FangSong_GB2312">对不具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同组在</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VWSHNM+FangSong_GB2312">过渡日的合同服务边际或未到期责任负债亏损部分采用修正追溯调</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VWSHNM+FangSong_GB2312">整法时，企业应当按照下列规定进行衔接处理：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VWSHNM+FangSong_GB2312">（一）以过渡日或更早日期（如适用）估计的未来现金流量为基础，根据合同组初始确认时至过渡日或更早日期（如适用）发生的现金流量进行调整，确定合同组在初始确认时的未来现金流量；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VWSHNM+FangSong_GB2312">（二）基于过渡日前最近至少三个会计年度可观察数据，考虑该数据与本准则第二十五条规定的折现率的相似性或差异，采用适当方法确定合同组在初始确认时或以后的折现率；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VWSHNM+FangSong_GB2312">（三）以过渡日估计的非金融风险调整金额为基础，根据在过</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VWSHNM+FangSong_GB2312">渡日签发或分出的类似保险合同的相关风险释放方式，估计过渡日之前合同组非金融风险调整的变动金额，确定合同组在初始确认时</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VWSHNM+FangSong_GB2312">的非金融风险调整金额；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VWSHNM+FangSong_GB2312">（四）采用与过渡日后一致的方法将过渡日前已付或应付的保</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VWSHNM+FangSong_GB2312">险获取现金流量系统合理地分摊至过渡日确认和预计将于过渡日后确认的合同组，分别调整过渡日合同服务边际和确认为保险获取现金流量资产。企业无法获得合理可靠的信息进行上述处理的，则不</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VWSHNM+FangSong_GB2312">应调整合同服务边际或确认保险获取现金流量资产；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VWSHNM+FangSong_GB2312">（五）合同组在初始确认时根据本条（一）至（四）确认合同</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VWSHNM+FangSong_GB2312">服务边际的，应当按照本条（二）确定的初始确认时折现率计提利息，并基于过渡日合同组中的剩余责任单元和该日前的责任单元，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VWSHNM+FangSong_GB2312">确定过渡日前计入损益的合同服务边际；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: VWSHNM+FangSong_GB2312">（六）合同组在初始确认时根据本条（一）至（四）确认未到</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">期责任负债亏损部分的，应当采用系统合理的方法，确定分摊至过</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">渡日前的亏损部分；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">（七）对于订立时点不晚于对应的亏损保险合同确认时点的分</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">出的再保险合同，应当根据过渡日对应的亏损保险合同的未到期责任负债亏损部分乘以预计从分出的再保险合同组摊回的对应的保险合同赔付的比例，计算分出再保险合同组分保摊回未到期责任资产在过渡日的亏损摊回部分金额，企业无法获得合理可靠的信息确定</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">该亏损摊回部分金额的，则不应确认亏损摊回部分。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百一十一条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">对具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同组在</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">过渡日的合同服务边际或未到期责任负债亏损部分采用修正追溯调</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">整法时，企业应当按照下列规定进行衔接处理：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">（一）以过渡日基础项目公允价值减去该日履约现金流量的金</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">额为基础，根据过渡日前相关现金流量以及非金融风险调整的变动</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">进行恰当调整；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">（二）采用与过渡日后一致的方法将过渡日前已付或应付的保</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">险获取现金流量系统合理地分摊至过渡日确认和预计将于过渡日后确认的合同组，分别调整过渡日合同服务边际和确认为保险获取现金流量资产。企业无法获得合理可靠的信息进行上述处理的，则不</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">应调整合同服务边际或确认保险获取现金流量资产；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">（三）合同组根据本条（一）和（二）确认合同服务边际的，应当基于过渡日合同组中的剩余责任单元和该日前的责任单元，确</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">定过渡日前计入损益的合同服务边际；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: IPWHLV+FangSong_GB2312">（四）合同组根据本条（一）和（二）确认未到期责任负债亏</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OQBIDT+FangSong_GB2312">损部分的，应当将该亏损部分调整为零，同时将该亏损部分增加过</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OQBIDT+FangSong_GB2312">渡日未到期责任负债账面价值。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百一十二条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OQBIDT+FangSong_GB2312">企业对过渡日保险合同金融变动额采用修</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OQBIDT+FangSong_GB2312">正追溯调整法时，应当按照下列规定进行衔接处理：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OQBIDT+FangSong_GB2312">（一）根据本准则第一百零九条（一）规定将签发或分出时间相隔超过一年的合同归入同一合同组的，可以在过渡日确定合同组初始确认时或以后适用的折现率。企业根据本准则第三十四条选择将保险合同金融变动额分解计入保险财务损益和其他综合收益的，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OQBIDT+FangSong_GB2312">应当采用适当方法确定过渡日计入其他综合收益的累计金额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OQBIDT+FangSong_GB2312">（二）未将签发或分出时间相隔超过一年的合同归入同一合同组的，应当按照本准则第一百一十条（二）估计合同组初始确认时或以后适用的折现率。企业根据本准则第三十四条选择将保险合同金融变动额分解计入保险财务损益和计入其他综合收益的，应当采</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OQBIDT+FangSong_GB2312">用适当方法确定过渡日计入其他综合收益的累计金额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百一十三条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OQBIDT+FangSong_GB2312">企业根据本准则第三十七条规定选择不调</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OQBIDT+FangSong_GB2312">整中期财务报表有关会计估计处理结果的会计政策的，应当在过渡日对该会计政策采用追溯调整法处理。采用追溯调整法不切实可行的，企业可以采用修正追溯调整法，对保险合同金融变动额和不具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同的合同服务边际或未到期责任负债</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OQBIDT+FangSong_GB2312">亏损部分进行衔接处理时，视同过渡日前未编制中期财务报表。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百一十四条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OQBIDT+FangSong_GB2312">企业采用公允价值法时，可以使用在合同</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: OQBIDT+FangSong_GB2312">开始日或初始确认时根据合同条款和市场状况可确定的合理可靠的信息，或使用在过渡日可获得的合理可靠的信息，根据本准则规定</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">识别下列事项并进行衔接处理：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">（一）保险合同组，企业可以将签发或分出时间间隔超过一年</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">的合同归入同一合同组；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">（二）具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">（三）不具有直接参与分红特征的保险合同中的相机抉择现金</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">流量；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN
