style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">（四）具有相机参与分红特征的投资合同。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">企业采用公允价值法时，对于在合同转让或非同一控制下企业合并中取得的保险合同，可以将该类合同在转让日或购买日前已发</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">生的赔付义务确认为已发生赔款负债。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百一十五条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">企业采用公允价值法时，按照下列规定进</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">行衔接处理：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">（一）企业可以在过渡日确定合同组初始确认时或以后适用的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">折现率；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">（二）对于分出的再保险合同组对应亏损保险合同的，应当根</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">据过渡日对应的亏损保险合同的未到期责任负债亏损部分乘以预计从分出的再保险合同组摊回的对应的保险合同赔付的比例，计算分出再保险合同组分保摊回未到期责任资产在过渡日的亏损摊回部分</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">金额；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">（三）企业根据本准则第三十四条选择将保险合同金融变动额</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">分解计入保险财务损益和其他综合收益的，应当采用适当方法确定</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">过渡日计入其他综合收益的累计金额；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: KILWAD+FangSong_GB2312">（四）对保险获取现金流量资产采用追溯调整法不切实可行时，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当采用适当方法确定过渡日的保险获取现金流量资产。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百一十六条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当在附注中披露与衔接处理相关的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">（一）在采用修正追溯调整法和公允价值法的保险合同的存续</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">期间，说明该类保险合同在过渡日的衔接处理；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">（二）在本准则第八十六条和第八十七条规定的调节表中，分别就过渡日采用修正追溯调整法和公允价值法的保险合同，在该类保险合同存续期间单独披露其对保险服务收入和合同服务边际的影</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">响；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">（三）企业根据本准则第一百一十二条和第一百一十五条（三）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">的规定，采用修正追溯调整法或公允价值法确定过渡日计入其他综合收益的累计金额的，在该金额减计为零之前的期间，应当披露以公允价值计量且其变动计入其他综合收益的相关金融资产计入其他</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">综合收益的累计金额自期初至期末的调节情况。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百一十七条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">企业无须披露比首次执行日前最近一个会</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">计年度更早期间的信息。企业选择披露未经调整的更早期间的比较</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">信息的，应当列示该类信息并说明其编制基础。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">企业可以选择不披露未公开的、比首次执行日前四个会计年度</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">更早期间发生的索赔进展情况，但应当披露这一选择。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百一十八条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">企业在本准则首次执行日前执行金融工具</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">相关会计准则的，应当在本准则首次执行日对金融资产进行下列处</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">理：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: QLCBDG+FangSong_GB2312">（一）企业可以对管理金融资产的业务模式进行重新评估并确</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">定金融资产分类，但为了与本准则适用范围内合同无关的活动而持</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">有的金融资产除外；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">（二）在首次执行日前被指定为以公允价值计量且其变动计入</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">当期损益的金融资产，因企业执行本准则而不再符合指定条件时，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">应当撤销之前的指定；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">（三）金融资产因企业执行本准则而符合指定条件的，可以指</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">定为以公允价值计量且其变动计入当期损益的金融资产；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">（四）企业可以将非交易性权益工具投资指定为以公允价值计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">量且其变动计入其他综合收益的金融资产或撤销之前的指定。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">企业应当以本准则首次执行日的事实和情况为基础进行上述处</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">理，并追溯调整首次执行本准则当年年初留存收益或权益的其他部分。企业无须调整可比期间信息。企业选择调整可比期间信息的，应当以前期事实和情况为基础，以反映金融工具相关会计准则的要</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">求。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百一十九条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">企业根据本准则第一百一十八条规定进行</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">处理的，应当披露下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">（一）根据本准则第一百一十八条（一）对管理相关金融资产</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">的业务模式进行重新评估并确定金融资产分类的标准；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">（二）相关金融资产列报类型和账面价值的变化；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">（三）撤销之前指定为以公允价值计量且其变动计入当期损益</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">的金融资产的期末账面价值；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">（四）指定或撤销指定以公允价值计量且其变动计入当期损益</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: DVJJMT+FangSong_GB2312">的相关金融资产的原因。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第十一章</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 11.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">附则</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormalCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第一百二十条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 24.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EQOPPH+FangSong_GB2312">本准则自</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">2023<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EQOPPH+FangSong_GB2312">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">1<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EQOPPH+FangSong_GB2312">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"> 
</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">1<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: EQOPPH+FangSong_GB2312">日起施行。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P>
